3. The place is large, but the road signs are messy and unclear. I went around three or four times to find a children's play center but couldn't find it
4. Are there separate charges for riding a bike and swimming pool? I came here after watching a short video of a travel blogger. He told me that they charge a fee. Why didn't they explain it when they advertised it?
5. It's too far from the center of Xuzhou. The taxi fare is 30 or 40 yuan. There is no subway nearby. If you want to travel quickly and easily, don't consider this place.
Finally, why do I give all five stars? Because we left wonderful memories here with our children. These memories are worth five stars! Just take a look at the previous suggestions. I don't know if they will improve.
